\n558: \tchildren, subCtx := errgroup.WithContext(ctx)\n559: \n560: \tchildren.Go(func() error {\n561: \t\treturn ng.MultiOrgAlertmanager.Run(subCtx)\n562: \t})\n563: \tchildren.Go(func() error \"pkg/services/ngalert/state/historian/core.go\",\n      \"symbol\": \"RecordStateTransition\"\n    }\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"## Grafana Unified Alerting (ngalert) Architecture\\n\\n### Overview\\nThe Grafana unified alerting (ngalert) subsystem is composed of five major interconnected components that work together to evaluate alert rules, track their state, and send notifications. The system is orchestrated by the main AlertNG service defined in pkg/services/ngalert/ngalert.go.\\n\\n### 1. Alert Rule Storage (Store Layer)\\n**Primary Files:**\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/store/alert_rule.go` - Alert rule CRUD operations (DeleteAlertRulesByUID, InsertAlertRules, UpdateAlertRules)\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/store/database.go` - Main DBstore implementation with database transaction handling\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/store/models.go` - Database models for alertRule and alertRuleVersion tables\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/store/instance_database.go` - Alert instance storage for both simple and proto-based formats\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/store/proto_instance_database.go` - Protobuf-based alert instance storage\\n\\n**Key Classes:**\\n- `DBstore` - Central database abstraction providing access to alert rules, instances, and state\\n\\nThe store layer persists alert rule definitions in the database and manages alert instance state. It supports two storage backends for alert instances: a simple JSON-based format and a compressed protobuf format (controlled by feature flag alertingSaveStateCompressed).\\n\\n### 2. Scheduler (Evaluation Engine)\\n**Primary Files:**\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/schedule.go` - Main scheduler orchestrator that periodically evaluates alert rules\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/alert_rule.go` - Individual alert rule evaluation routine (alertRule type)\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/registry.go` - Maintains registry of active rule evaluation routines\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/fetcher.go` - Fetches alert rules from the store for scheduling\\n\\n**Key Classes:**\\n- `schedule` - Main scheduler struct that runs the periodic evaluation loop (Run method)\\n- `alertRule` - Represents an individual running alert rule with its evaluation routine\\n- `ruleRegistry` - Thread-safe registry of active alert rule evaluation routines\\n- `ScheduleService` - Interface for the scheduler service\\n- `RulesStore` - Interface for fetching rules (GetAlertRulesKeysForScheduling, GetAlertRulesForScheduling)\\n- `AlertsSender` - Interface for sending alerts to the notifier (implemented by AlertsRouter)\\n\\n**Data Flow:**\\nThe scheduler's Run method calls schedulePeriodic, which processes ticks at a base interval. For each tick, processTick:\\n1. Fetches the current set of alert rules from the store\\n2. Determines which rules are ready to run based on their evaluation interval\\n3. Creates evaluation routines for new rules\\n4. Sends ready-to-run evaluations to alert rule routines\\n5. Cleans up deleted rules\\n\\n### 3. State Manager\\n**Primary Files:**\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/state/manager.go` - Central state management (Manager type)\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/state/state.go` - Alert instance state representation (State type)\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/state/cache.go` - In-memory state cache for fast lookups\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/state/persist.go` - State persistence abstraction (StatePersister interface)\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/state/persister_sync.go` - Synchronous state persistence\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/state/persister_async.go` - Asynchronous periodic state persistence\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/state/persister_noop.go` - No-op persister for disabled state saving\\n\\n**Key Classes:**\\n- `Manager` - Manages alert instance states, provides ProcessEvalResults and GetAll methods\\n- `State` - Represents an alert instance state with health status\\n- `cache` - In-memory cache of alert instances, keyed by (orgID, ruleUID)\\n- `StatePersister` - Interface with Sync and Async methods for persisting states\\n- `AlertInstanceManager` - Interface for querying current alert instances\\n- `syncStatePersister` - Persists states synchronously to the database\\n- `asyncStatePersister` - Periodically collects and persists states asynchronously\\n\\n**Data Flow:**\\nAfter alert rules are evaluated by the scheduler, the results flow to the state manager:\\n1. The scheduler calls alertRule.Eval with evaluation results\\n2. This triggers stateManager.ProcessEvalResults\\n3. The state manager updates the in-memory cache with new alert states\\n4. Based on the configured StatePersister, states are saved to the database (synchronously, asynchronously, or not at all)\\n5. State transitions are recorded to the historian\\n\\n### 4. Notifier (Alert Routing & Notification)\\n**Primary Files:**\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/multiorg_alertmanager.go` - Multi-organization alertmanager orchestrator\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/alertmanager.go` - Individual organization alertmanager implementation\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/config.go` - Alertmanager configuration management\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/alerts.go` - Alert data structures and handling\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/sender/router.go` - Alerts router that determines where to send alerts\\n\\n**Key Classes:**\\n- `MultiOrgAlertmanager` - Manages per-organization alertmanager instances\\n- `Alertmanager` - Interface for individual alertmanager operations (ApplyConfig, PutAlerts, GetAlerts, etc.)\\n- `AlertsRouter` - Routes alerts from the scheduler to either internal or external alertmanagers\\n- `AlertsSender` - Interface implemented by AlertsRouter.Send method\\n\\n**Data Flow:**\\nAfter state transitions occur and new alert instances need to be notified:\\n1. The scheduler calls AlertsRouter.Send(context, ruleKey, alerts)\\n2. AlertsRouter checks admin configuration to determine if alerts should go to internal or external alertmanagers\\n3. For internal alertmanager: AlertsRouter calls MultiOrgAlertmanager.PutAlerts\\n4. MultiOrgAlertmanager routes to the appropriate organization's Alertmanager instance\\n5. The Alertmanager applies notification rules, silences, and grouping\\n6. Alerts are sent to configured contact points (email, Slack, PagerDuty, etc.)\\n\\nThe notifier also supports remote alertmanager modes:\\n- Remote Primary: Grafana's alertmanager is a remote instance\\n- Remote Secondary: Syncs with a remote alertmanager while maintaining local state\\n\\n### 5. History Writer (State Transition Recording)\\n**Primary Files:**\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/state/historian/core.go` - Core historian logic with shouldRecord decision logic\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/state/historian/backend.go` - Backend abstraction for history storage\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/state/historian/annotation.go` - Stores history as Grafana annotations\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/state/historian/loki.go` - Stores history in remote Loki instance\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/state/historian/prometheus.go` - Stores history as metrics in remote Prometheus/Mimir\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/state/historian/multiple.go` - Supports writing to multiple backends simultaneously\\n\\n**Key Classes:**\\n- `Backend` - Interface for history storage implementations\\n- `AnnotationBackend` - Stores alert state transitions as dashboard annotations\\n- `RemoteLokiBackend` - Sends alert state history to remote Loki for log-based history\\n- `RemotePrometheusBackend` - Sends alert state history as time series metrics to remote Prometheus/Mimir\\n- `MultipleBackend` - Writes state transitions to both primary and secondary backends\\n\\n**Data Flow:**\\nWhen alert state transitions occur:\\n1. StateTransition events are passed to the Historian.RecordStateTransition method\\n2. The historian evaluates shouldRecord logic to determine if the transition should be recorded\\n3. Based on the configured backend:\\n   - Annotations: Creates or updates dashboard annotations\\n   - Loki: Sends logs with alert state metadata\\n   - Prometheus: Writes metrics (e.g., ALERTS state tracking)\\n   - Multiple: Records to all configured backends for redundancy\\n\\n### 6. Evaluator (Condition Evaluation)\\n**Primary Files:**\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/eval/eval.go` - Alert condition evaluation engine\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/eval/factory.go` - Factory for creating evaluators\\n\\n**Key Classes:**\\n- `ConditionEvaluator` - Interface with EvaluateRaw and Evaluate methods\\n- `conditionEvaluator` - Executes query pipelines and converts responses to alert states\\n- `EvaluatorFactory` - Creates evaluators from condition definitions\\n\\nThe evaluator executes the alert rule's condition (which may include data source queries and expressions) and determines whether the rule should alert.\\n\\n### 7. Recording Rules Writer\\n**Primary Files:**\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/writer/prom.go` - Prometheus remote write implementation\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/writer/datasourcewriter.go` - Datasource-agnostic remote writer\\n\\n**Key Classes:**\\n- `PrometheusWriter` - Writes recording rule results via Prometheus remote write protocol\\n- `DatasourceWriter` - Writes metric data to configured datasources\\n\\n### 8. Data Models\\n**Primary Files:**\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/models/alert_rule.go` - AlertRule type and related structures\\n\\n**Key Classes:**\\n- `AlertRule` - Represents an alert rule with UID, interval, data source queries, condition, and notification settings\\n- `AlertRuleKey` - Unique identifier for an alert rule (OrgID + UID)\\n\\n### 9. API Layer\\n**Primary Files:**\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/api/api.go` - Main API struct\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/api/api_alerting.go` - Alert-related endpoints\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/api/api_provisioning.go` - Provisioning endpoints\\n\\n### System Integration\\n\\n**Main Service Initialization (ngalert.go::ProvideService):**\\nThe AlertNG service orchestrates all components:\\n1. Initializes the database store (DBstore)\\n2. Creates the evaluator factory\\n3. Sets up the state manager with configured persister\\n4. Creates the scheduler and state manager\\n5. Initializes the MultiOrgAlertmanager and AlertsRouter\\n6. Configures the historian backend(s)\\n7. Sets up the recording rules writer\\n8. Registers API endpoints\\n\\n**Execution Flow (ngalert.go::Run):**\\n1. Starts MultiOrgAlertmanager (manages alertmanager lifecycle)\\n2. Starts AlertsRouter (syncs admin configuration)\\n3. If ExecuteAlerts is enabled:\\n   - Warms up the state manager cache from database\\n   - Starts the scheduler (evaluates rules periodically)\\n   - Starts the state manager (persists state changes, records history)\\n\\n**Configuration Control:**\\n- Feature flags control: state storage format (compressed vs. simple), state persistence mode (sync/async/none), remote alertmanager mode\\n- Config settings control: base evaluation interval, minimum rule interval, recording rules, state history backend, notification history backend\\n\\n### Key Design Patterns\\n\\n1. **Multi-Organization Support**: MultiOrgAlertmanager creates separate alertmanager instances per organization\\n2. **Pluggable Persistence**: StatePersister interface allows different persistence strategies\\n3. **Pluggable History**: Backend interface allows storing state history in different systems\\n4. **Registry Pattern**: ruleRegistry and alertRulesRegistry maintain active rules\\n5. **Factory Pattern**: EvaluatorFactory creates condition evaluators, alertmanager factory creates alertmanagers\\n6. **Strategy Pattern**: Different alertmanager implementations (remote primary, remote secondary, local)\\n7. **Event-Driven**: State transitions trigger historian callbacks and notification attempts\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":13,"cache_creation_input_tokens":7689,"cache_read_input_tokens":83730,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":7689},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"f6a5f6fe-194c-49c5-b470-167ea0e9be35","uuid":"9f1a4864-f1bd-4fad-aef4-12a17dbe3bb3"}

Grafana unified alerting (ngalert) subsystem is composed of five major interconnected components that work together to evaluate alert rules, track their state, and send notifications. The system is orchestrated by the main AlertNG service defined in pkg/services/ngalert/ngalert.go.\\n\\n### 1. Alert Rule Storage (Store Layer)\\n**Primary Files:**\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/store/alert_rule.go` - Alert rule CRUD operations (DeleteAlertRulesByUID, InsertAlertRules, UpdateAlertRules)\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/store/database.go` - Main DBstore implementation with database transaction handling\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/store/models.go` - Database models for alertRule and alertRuleVersion tables\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/store/instance_database.go` - Alert instance storage for both simple and proto-based formats\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/store/proto_instance_database.go` - Protobuf-based alert instance storage\\n\\n**Key Classes:**\\n- `DBstore` - Central database abstraction providing access to alert rules, instances, and state\\n\\nThe store layer persists alert rule definitions in the database and manages alert instance state. It supports two storage backends for alert instances: a simple JSON-based format and a compressed protobuf format (controlled by feature flag alertingSaveStateCompressed).\\n\\n### 2. Scheduler (Evaluation Engine)\\n**Primary Files:**\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/schedule.go` - Main scheduler orchestrator that periodically evaluates alert rules\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/alert_rule.go` - Individual alert rule evaluation routine (alertRule type)\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/registry.go` - Maintains registry of active rule evaluation routines\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/fetcher.go` - Fetches alert rules from the store for scheduling\\n\\n**Key Classes:**\\n- `schedule` - Main scheduler struct that runs the periodic evaluation loop (Run method)\\n- `alertRule` - Represents an individual running alert rule with its evaluation routine\\n- `ruleRegistry` - Thread-safe registry of active alert rule evaluation routines\\n- `ScheduleService` - Interface for the scheduler service\\n- `RulesStore` - Interface for fetching rules (GetAlertRulesKeysForScheduling, GetAlertRulesForScheduling)\\n- `AlertsSender` - Interface for sending alerts to the notifier (implemented by AlertsRouter)\\n\\n**Data Flow:**\\nThe scheduler's Run method calls schedulePeriodic, which processes ticks at a base interval. For each tick, processTick:\\n1. Fetches the current set of alert rules from the store\\n2. Determines which rules are ready to run based on their evaluation interval\\n3. Creates evaluation routines for new rules\\n4. Sends ready-to-run evaluations to alert rule routines\\n5. Cleans up deleted rules\\n\\n### 3. State Manager\\n**Primary Files:**\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/state/manager.go` - Central state management (Manager type)\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/state/state.go` - Alert instance state representation (State type)\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/state/cache.go` - In-memory state cache for fast lookups\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/state/persist.go` - State persistence abstraction (StatePersister interface)\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/state/persister_sync.go` - Synchronous state persistence\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/state/persister_async.go` - Asynchronous periodic state persistence\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/state/persister_noop.go` - No-op persister for disabled state saving\\n\\n**Key Classes:**\\n- `Manager` - Manages alert instance states, provides ProcessEvalResults and GetAll methods\\n- `State` - Represents an alert instance state with health status\\n- `cache` - In-memory cache of alert instances, keyed by (orgID, ruleUID)\\n- `StatePersister` - Interface with Sync and Async methods for persisting states\\n- `AlertInstanceManager` - Interface for querying current alert instances\\n- `syncStatePersister` - Persists states synchronously to the database\\n- `asyncStatePersister` - Periodically collects and persists states asynchronously\\n\\n**Data Flow:**\\nAfter alert rules are evaluated by the scheduler, the results flow to the state manager:\\n1. The scheduler calls alertRule.Eval with evaluation results\\n2. This triggers stateManager.ProcessEvalResults\\n3. The state manager updates the in-memory cache with new alert states\\n4. Based on the configured StatePersister, states are saved to the database (synchronously, asynchronously, or not at all)\\n5. State transitions are recorded to the historian\\n\\n### 4. Notifier (Alert Routing & Notification)\\n**Primary Files:**\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/multiorg_alertmanager.go` - Multi-organization alertmanager orchestrator\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/alertmanager.go` - Individual organization alertmanager implementation\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/config.go` - Alertmanager configuration management\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/alerts.go` - Alert data structures and handling\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/sender/router.go` - Alerts router that determines where to send alerts\\n\\n**Key Classes:**\\n- `MultiOrgAlertmanager` - Manages per-organization alertmanager instances\\n- `Alertmanager` - Interface for individual alertmanager operations (ApplyConfig, PutAlerts, GetAlerts, etc.)\\n- `AlertsRouter` - Routes alerts from the scheduler to either internal or external alertmanagers\\n- `AlertsSender` - Interface implemented by AlertsRouter.Send method\\n\\n**Data Flow:**\\nAfter state transitions occur and new alert instances need to be notified:\\n1. The scheduler calls AlertsRouter.Send(context, ruleKey, alerts)\\n2. AlertsRouter checks admin configuration to determine if alerts should go to internal or external alertmanagers\\n3. For internal alertmanager: AlertsRouter calls MultiOrgAlertmanager.PutAlerts\\n4. MultiOrgAlertmanager routes to the appropriate organization's Alertmanager instance\\n5. The Alertmanager applies notification rules, silences, and grouping\\n6. Alerts are sent to configured contact points (email, Slack, PagerDuty, etc.)\\n\\nThe notifier also supports remote alertmanager modes:\\n- Remote Primary: Grafana's alertmanager is a remote instance\\n- Remote Secondary: Syncs with a remote alertmanager while maintaining local state\\n\\n### 5. History Writer (State Transition Recording)\\n**Primary Files:**\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/state/historian/core.go` - Core historian logic with shouldRecord decision logic\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/state/historian/backend.go` - Backend abstraction for history storage\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/state/historian/annotation.go` - Stores history as Grafana annotations\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/state/historian/loki.go` - Stores history in remote Loki instance\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/state/historian/prometheus.go` - Stores history as metrics in remote Prometheus/Mimir\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/state/historian/multiple.go` - Supports writing to multiple backends simultaneously\\n\\n**Key Classes:**\\n- `Backend` - Interface for history storage implementations\\n- `AnnotationBackend` - Stores alert state transitions as dashboard annotations\\n- `RemoteLokiBackend` - Sends alert state history to remote Loki for log-based history\\n- `RemotePrometheusBackend` - Sends alert state history as time series metrics to remote Prometheus/Mimir\\n- `MultipleBackend` - Writes state transitions to both primary and secondary backends\\n\\n**Data Flow:**\\nWhen alert state transitions occur:\\n1. StateTransition events are passed to the Historian.RecordStateTransition method\\n2. The historian evaluates shouldRecord logic to determine if the transition should be recorded\\n3. Based on the configured backend:\\n   - Annotations: Creates or updates dashboard annotations\\n   - Loki: Sends logs with alert state metadata\\n   - Prometheus: Writes metrics (e.g., ALERTS state tracking)\\n   - Multiple: Records to all configured backends for redundancy\\n\\n### 6. Evaluator (Condition Evaluation)\\n**Primary Files:**\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/eval/eval.go` - Alert condition evaluation engine\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/eval/factory.go` - Factory for creating evaluators\\n\\n**Key Classes:**\\n- `ConditionEvaluator` - Interface with EvaluateRaw and Evaluate methods\\n- `conditionEvaluator` - Executes query pipelines and converts responses to alert states\\n- `EvaluatorFactory` - Creates evaluators from condition definitions\\n\\nThe evaluator executes the alert rule's condition (which may include data source queries and expressions) and determines whether the rule should alert.\\n\\n### 7. Recording Rules Writer\\n**Primary Files:**\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/writer/prom.go` - Prometheus remote write implementation\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/writer/datasourcewriter.go` - Datasource-agnostic remote writer\\n\\n**Key Classes:**\\n- `PrometheusWriter` - Writes recording rule results via Prometheus remote write protocol\\n- `DatasourceWriter` - Writes metric data to configured datasources\\n\\n### 8. Data Models\\n**Primary Files:**\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/models/alert_rule.go` - AlertRule type and related structures\\n\\n**Key Classes:**\\n- `AlertRule` - Represents an alert rule with UID, interval, data source queries, condition, and notification settings\\n- `AlertRuleKey` - Unique identifier for an alert rule (OrgID + UID)\\n\\n### 9. API Layer\\n**Primary Files:**\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/api/api.go` - Main API struct\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/api/api_alerting.go` - Alert-related endpoints\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/api/api_provisioning.go` - Provisioning endpoints\\n\\n### System Integration\\n\\n**Main Service Initialization (ngalert.go::ProvideService):**\\nThe AlertNG service orchestrates all components:\\n1. Initializes the database store (DBstore)\\n2. Creates the evaluator factory\\n3. Sets up the state manager with configured persister\\n4. Creates the scheduler and state manager\\n5. Initializes the MultiOrgAlertmanager and AlertsRouter\\n6. Configures the historian backend(s)\\n7. Sets up the recording rules writer\\n8. Registers API endpoints\\n\\n**Execution Flow (ngalert.go::Run):**\\n1. Starts MultiOrgAlertmanager (manages alertmanager lifecycle)\\n2. Starts AlertsRouter (syncs admin configuration)\\n3. If ExecuteAlerts is enabled:\\n   - Warms up the state manager cache from database\\n   - Starts the scheduler (evaluates rules periodically)\\n   - Starts the state manager (persists state changes, records history)\\n\\n**Configuration Control:**\\n- Feature flags control: state storage format (compressed vs. simple), state persistence mode (sync/async/none), remote alertmanager mode\\n- Config settings control: base evaluation interval, minimum rule interval, recording rules, state history backend, notification history backend\\n\\n### Key Design Patterns\\n\\n1. **Multi-Organization Support**: MultiOrgAlertmanager creates separate alertmanager instances per organization\\n2. **Pluggable Persistence**: StatePersister interface allows different persistence strategies\\n3. **Pluggable History**: Backend interface allows storing state history in different systems\\n4. **Registry Pattern**: ruleRegistry and alertRulesRegistry maintain active rules\\n5. **Factory Pattern**: EvaluatorFactory creates condition evaluators, alertmanager factory creates alertmanagers\\n6. **Strategy Pattern**: Different alertmanager implementations (remote primary, remote secondary, local)\\n7. **Event-Driven**: State transitions trigger historian callbacks and notification attempts\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
